FROM [Categories] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Name], CASE
        WHEN (([t0].[Date] = @__daydate_1) AND ([t0].[Date] IS NOT NULL AND @__daydate_1 IS NOT NULL)) OR ([t0].[Date] IS NULL AND @__daydate_1 IS NULL) THEN [t0].[Quantity]
        ELSE 0
    END AS [c], [d].[PictureId], [d].[CategoriesId], [t].[Date], [t].[DishId], [t].[CompanyId]
    FROM [Dishes] AS [d]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [d0].[Date], [d0].[DishId], [d0].[CompanyId]
        FROM [DayDish] AS [d0]
        WHERE (([d0].[CompanyId] = @__companyid_0) AND @__companyid_0 IS NOT NULL) AND (([d0].[Date] = @__daydate_1) AND @__daydate_1 IS NOT NULL)
    ) AS [t] ON [d].[Id] = [t].[DishId]

FROM [Categories] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Name], CASE
        WHEN (([t0].[Date] = @__daydate_1) AND ([t0].[Date] IS NOT NULL AND @__daydate_1 IS NOT NULL)) OR ([t0].[Date] IS NULL AND @__daydate_1 IS NULL) THEN [t0].[Quantity]
        ELSE 0
    END AS [c], [d].[PictureId], [d].[CategoriesId], [t].[Date], [t].[DishId], [t].[CompanyId]
    FROM [Dishes] AS [d]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [d0].[Date], [d0].[DishId], [d0].[CompanyId]
        FROM [DayDish] AS [d0]
        WHERE (([d0].[CompanyId] = @__companyid_0) AND @__companyid_0 IS NOT NULL) AND (([d0].[Date] = @__daydate_1) AND @__daydate_1 IS NOT NULL)
